Of course, this absurd thought only passed through Li’s mind once before he suppressed it deep within his consciousness.

He was well aware that he was not the reincarnation of some significant figure. As a cultivator, certain things could be ascertained...

So, why did Big Boss Tyrannical Song suddenly address him as ‘senior’? Being called that by Big Boss Tyrannical Song gave him a sensation of impending doom—he truly couldn’t bear such an esteemed title.

“Shuhang really hasn’t changed,” Venerable Yellow Mountain remarked with satisfaction as he glanced at Song Shuhang.

Although his level of cultivation had improved, his inherent nature remained unchanged. He was still the same kind-hearted young man he had been when he first joined the group.

This was quite rare. If someone else were like Song Shuhang, whose power had surged dramatically in a short period, it was very likely their mindset would expand to the point of being uncontrollable.

This is the relationship between Dao heart and strength. Powerful strength requires an equally formidable Dao heart to match.

Across from him, the virtuous lamia observed Venerable Yellow Mountain’s satisfied expression from afar and roughly guessed his thoughts—ever since she had learned to read Song Shuhangs expressions, she could occasionally deduce others’ thoughts from their apparent expressions.

‘In fact, Shuhangs mentality has always been sound, and there was basically no reason for him to become overly arrogant. Other than his personality... It’s probably because he has a group of exceedingly powerful items in his social circle,’ the virtuous lamia added internally.

Influenced by that group of exceedingly powerful items and his circle of friends, Song Shuhang managed to maintain his novice mentality. He never felt overly impressive and always considered himself quite green.

Of course, Song Shuhangs personality was also excellent. Regardless of his current level of cultivation, for him, the seniors in the ‘Nine Provinces Number One Group’ would always remain seniors. This fact would not change now or in the future.

With a smile, Song Shuhang approached Great Eastern Monarch and gave a respectful hand gesture.

“Let’s go,” Venerable Yellow Mountain gently nudged the bewildered Great Eastern Monarch, signaling him to snap out of it. At the same time, he used a secret voice transmission to instruct him to relay the coordinates of the ‘Spirit Transformation Ruins’ to Song Shuhang.

With Venerable Yellow Mountain’s prompting, Great Eastern Monarch finally regained his composure—and he realized that Tyrannical Song had discreetly assisted him out of trouble for Yellow Mountain’s sake.

Grateful, Great Eastern Monarch quickly used a secret sound transmission to describe the precise location of the ‘Spirit Transformation Ruins! to Song Shuhang.

After receiving the location, Song Shuhang briefly calculated the coordinates for spatial teleportation in his mind.

“Then, seniors, let’s set off.” After this, Song Shuhang clasped his fingers and gently tapped the air.

Bang—a crisp sound of shattering resonated through the space.

Subsequently, the spatial rift opened and transformed into a doorway of

space.

Song Shuhang was not yet proficient with the power of space, so after opening the spatial gate, he had to focus intently on maintaining the spatial passageway, allowing Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Monarch to enter first.

Following Song Shuhangs direction, Great Eastern Monarch first closed the door to his hidden cave abode and then stepped through the spatial gate with

Venerable Yellow Mountain, heading toward the Spirit Transformation Ruins.

‘F*ck, what happened today is enough to keep me cool for a hundred years!’ After entering the spatial gate, Great Eastern Monarch felt as if he had drunk too much wine, his whole being was floating.

Moreover, he didn’t even need to boast about it himself—a certain group of cultivators on the moon would inflate his coolness for him.

Of course, he couldn’t brag about it himself.

If Tyrannical Song had previously called him ‘Fellow Daoist,’ he could have personally boasted about being on the same level as Tyrannical Song.

However, since Tyrannical Song had helped him in secret by calling him ‘senior’... Then he couldn’t touch this cool topic.

He was a person aware of his own limits, and he was not truly Tyrannical Songs senior, so boasting would shorten his lifespan.

“Yellow Mountain, what exactly is your relationship with Big Boss Tyrannical Song?” Great Eastern Monarch asked curiously.

“I’ve told you before,” Mother Yellow Mountain replied calmly.

However, Mother Yellow Mountain’s heart was not as calm as his expression suggested.

He had noticed that Song Shuhang had opened the spatial gate by merely tapping his finger in the air.

In other words, Shuhang might have already mastered the ability to manipulate space?

Mother Yellow Mountain suddenly felt both gratified and exhausted—a very complex emotion.

He was gratified that his child had grown once more. The reason he felt exhausted was not something that could be explained in a few words.

At the entrance of the Spirit Transformation Ruins.

Great Eastern Monarch took out a disc- shaped magical artifact and pressed it into the air, opening the entrance to the Spirit Transformation Ruins.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, this is the Spirit Transformation Ruins... Of course, I actually came up with this name myself,” Great Eastern Monarch explained. “The real name of this ruin is recorded in the primordial language. I can’t read the information in the primordial language. Senior Tyrannical Song, have you studied ancient languages?” Great Eastern Monarch put away the disc and led Song Shuhang and Venerable Yellow Mountain into the ruins.

Song Shuhang smiled and shook his head.

I haven’t even mastered the ancient language, let alone the primordial language, Song Shuhang thought to himself. However, he did possess a law related to the origin of all languages... If it occasionally flashed, Song Shuhang would be able to recognize some of the primordial characters.

“Senior Yellow Mountain, have you studied ancient characters?” Song Shuhang then asked Venerable Yellow Mountain.

“The ancient language is too remote. I haven’t studied it much,” Venerable Yellow Mountain responded.

As they spoke, the three of them arrived in front of a huge stone tablet.

The stone tablet was engraved with five ancient runes. Each rune contained an aura that had been tempered through countless trials.

Song Shuhang looked up at these five ancient characters, memorizing them in his heart.

Unfortunately, the ‘laws’ within him were not triggered this time, and they did not translate these five words for Song Shuhang.

“Fairy Virtue, do you know them?” Song Shuhang asked.

The virtuous lamia materialized and shook her head. Then, she said in Song Shuhangs voice, “That’s a good question. It’s very profound, so... Fairy, why don’t you ask the miraculous Father Goudan?”

This was Song Shuhangs response to Cheng Goudan after his father changed his Daoist name.

This line was also recorded by the virtuous lamia.

“Yeah, why didn’t 1 think of that?” Song Shuhang initiated a private chat and connected to Senior Striped Dragon Two. “Father Goudan, do you have a moment? Can you help me understand what these five ancient characters mean?”

As he spoke, he sent five pictures of the ancient language over.

“What are you looking at? Get lost!” Father Goudan dismissed him mercilessly.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

“These five ancient characters mean ‘What are you looking at, scram,”‘ Fairy Cheng Goudan explained helpfully.

Song Shuhang was speechless..

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation   Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

So, Father Goudan had actually translated it for me before?

So, I can’t forget to thank him.

Song Shuhang took a deep breath and adjusted his state of mind, then replied,

“Thank you, Father Goudan!”

“You’re welcome. Next time you need to translate the Grand Ancient language, come to me again,” Father Goudan replied.

Song Shuhang raised his head and looked up at the sky. He felt as if he had been slapped in the face.

This fully showed how important it was to learn knowledge.

“Learning makes people happy. If you don’t study hard, you’ll suffer.” Song Shuhang sighed and said, “I’ll go and study the archaic characters later.”

Great Eastern Emperor was confused.

Was this Big Boss Tyrannical Songs lament?

Did the big shot feel that he was not working hard enough and wanted to continue learning all kinds of cultivation knowledge?

However, in today’s myriad worlds, in terms of cultivation knowledge alone, Tyrannical Song was already enough to rank in the top ten, right?

During the “Sexy Tyrannical Song, Answer Online” lecture, Big Boss Tyrannical Song had single-handedly answered almost all the questions raised by the fellow daoists watching the lecture. After all, there were thousands of cultivation systems in the universe, and each cultivation system had a completely different theoretical system foundation.

From the side, it could be seen how much cultivation knowledge Big Boss Tyrannical Song had mastered!

Even so, Big Boss Tyrannical Song still had to seize the time to learn.

As expected, a real master would never stop learning.

Great Eastern Emperor felt that he had been subdued by Big Boss Tyrannical Songs charisma!

He looked at Big Boss Tyrannical Song with admiration.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless. Although he didn’t know what his friend was thinking, he felt that he was in a state of ‘self-conquering.’

Should he pull him into the Nine Provinces Number One Group and make his worldview collapse?

Great Eastern Emperor had been exploring secret realms for the past few years and had been isolated from the outside world. Some time ago, he had finally come out of the mystic realm with great difficulty, but because the news had leaked, he was hiding everywhere. Therefore, Yellow Mountain didn’t have the chance to add him to the group.

“Shuhang, what is written on this?” Venerable Yellow Mountain asked.

Song Shuhang sighed and replied, “These five archaic characters mean ‘What are you looking at? Get lost!’ It means that the owner of this ruin must have a very bad taste.”

If it weren’t for the fact that he wanted to prevent Yellow Mountain from getting too tired, Song Shuhang would definitely have been mischievous. However, in order to take care of Yellow Mountain, whose heart was already riddled with holes, Song Shuhang restrained himself this time.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless.

Great Eastern Emperor was speechless.

As if Song Shuhang had read the meaning of the ancient characters, the huge stone tablet began to shine. The five characters on it were like little stars, shining brightly and looking especially mocking.

This flickering stone tablet made Song Shuhang think of his fellow Daoist Stone Tablet.

Thereupon, Song Shuhang stepped forward without hesitation and pressed his hands on the stone tablet. His long hair turned into 64 braided hands, which were pressed on all corners of the stone tablet. As his strength increased, the number of braided hands he could control also increased.

“Cheap love!” Song Shuhang shouted a very romantic name. In the next moment, his hands and the 64 braided hands started to dance crazily. It broke through the sonic boom in an instant. The speed of each ‘hand’ per second exceeded 100.

The radiance of the Blade Nurturing Technique turned into a dazzling radiance.

Under the light of love, the huge stone tablet trembled violently.

“What spell is this?” Great Eastern Emperor said in shock.

This gentleness was filled with the radiance of the emotion of ‘love,’ and it warmed people’s hearts. As expected of Big Boss Tyrannical Song, who had great merit, he actually had such a warm spell.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless. I don’t know how to explain it to you, but this is actually a very orthodox technique in the cultivation world, such as the Saber Nurturing Technique or the Sword Nurturing Technique, which is used to support the ‘one with the sword.’ But I don’t think you’ll believe me if I explain it this way.

Three seconds!

In just three seconds, Song Shuhang calmly withdrew his 64 braided hands and hands. Two seconds ago, Song Shuhang had thrown out 13,200 rounds of the Saber Nurturing Technique. He started to slow down at the end of the third second. He only released 814 Cheap Love, which was 14,014 rounds.

This was a secret technique that Song Shuhang had developed for Senior Mental Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword. It was called the ‘Saber Nurturing Technique: I’m about to die, I’m about to die’.

The next time Senior Mental Demon Scarlet Heaven Sword stabbed him in the heart like this, he would do the same.

Buzz

In front of him, the stone tablet engraved with five archaic characters began to vibrate.

It was as if he was infected by Tyrannical Songs love.

A moment later, the huge stone tablet began to move on its own. It slowly moved to the side. Finally, a secret passage was revealed.

This hidden secret passage was suppressed by the stone tablet, and even the divine sense of cultivators could not detect it!

“There’s actually a secret passage?” Song Shuhang was slightly stunned. Then, he turned around and said, “Senior Yellow Mountain, Dao Monarch Li, shall we go down and take a look?”

Generally speaking, the secret passages in the ruins were either some kind of shortcut to the treasure area or an area where special treasures were hidden.

Senior Tyrannical Song is awesome! Great Eastern Emperor was cheering for Song Shuhang in his heart.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless. How could this work?

Song Shuhangs actions this time really hurt his waist. He had lived for so long and had explored at least 800 ruins, but he had never encountered such a situation.

A moment later, Song Shuhang led the way in front. He was here to be a meat shield, so he naturally had to do his job well.

Venerable Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor followed behind him.

The secret passage looked very ordinary. Along the way, they did not find any hidden treasures.

“Looks like it’s a shortcut to the depths of the mystic realm?” Song Shuhang said. He was walking slowly in front of them, and the virtuous lamia was secretly prepared. If there was an accident, she would immediately rush out and protect everyone.

After walking about 500 steps...

“Shuhang, wait.” Behind him, Senior Yellow Mountain’s panting could be heard.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, please slow down.” Great Eastern Emperor’s voice trembled as well.

Song Shuhang turned around and saw Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor looking very tired.

Song Shuhang was confused.

“This tunnel is a little strange. Every step I take is tempering my body,” Venerable Yellow Mountain said.

Even with his physique as a Seventh Stage Venerable, he was still panting after taking only 500 steps. Great Eastern Emperor, who was at the peak of the Sixth Stage Realm, was already exhausted.

“Tempered body? Is there such an effect?” Song Shuhang stretched his muscles and bones but didn’t feel anything.

Yellow Mountain was speechless. He suddenly felt so tired that he didn’t want to talk.

“If I’m not wrong, this passageway might be a rare body tempering treasure land in ancient times, the Immortal Body Passage,” Yellow Mountain explained after panting for a while.

“Is it something good?” Song Shuhang asked.

If it was something good, why not dig it out and move it to his Inner World?

Nine Serenities, Three Feet of Digging, Tradition and Domination..

“Once a cultivator reaches the Second Stage Realm, if they encounter an opportunity, they will be able to condense special physiques of different attributes. The Dao Sect was known as the Immortal Body, and there were more than ten types of Immortal Bodies in the Dao Sect. Correspondingly, fiendish cultivators had fiendish bodies, Buddhist cultivators had Buddhist seeds, Confucian sects had Confucian roots, and demonic cultivators had demonic bodies. However, it’s not easy to condense an immortal body, and the failure rate is ridiculously high.” Venerable Yellow Mountain explained.

“It sounds very powerful.” Song Shuhang humbly asked for advice.

On the side, Great Eastern Emperor looked at Big Boss Tyrannical Song with some doubt. Why didn’t the erudite Senior Tyrannical Song know anything about the ‘immortal body’? This wasn’t some profound knowledge, right? Even some small cultivation families had records of ‘immortal body’.

Perhaps it was because Senior Tyrannical Song was a figure from the ancient times, so some of his knowledge was different from that of the current cultivators?

“In the main world, some cultivation families or large sects with long inheritances have some methods to condense immortal bodies and devil bodies. And this Immortal Body Passage is one of the methods to condense an Immortal Body.” Venerable Yellow Mountain explained.

“That’s not right, Yellow Mountain. If it’s a method to condense an immortal body, why does it give us such a heavy pressure?” Great Eastern Emperor couldn’t help but ask.

He could begin condensing his immortal body after reaching the Second Stage Realm.

On the other hand, he and Yellow Mountain were existences of the Sixth or Seventh Stage Realm...There was no reason for a passage of the Second Stage to condense an immortal body to give them such a heavy pressure after 500 steps.

“That’s why I said that this is a precious ‘body refining treasure’. In ancient times, this immortal body passageway, coupled with special cultivation techniques, medicinal herbs, treasures, and heavenly flames, could allow disciples to have a chance to condense an immortal body. Other than that, it was also a precious place for body refinement. For cultivators who cultivate body tempering techniques, just a short journey here can have a supreme body tempering effect.” Venerable Yellow Mountain said.

“That’s great.” Song Shuhang gave him a thumbs up.

He was worrying about how to teach his disciples to cultivate. After all, his own cultivation experience was very difficult to match with his disciples.

This Immortal Body Passage was simply a timely help to him.

After he taught his disciples the Holy Ape Dragon Power Technique, he would let them walk around the Immortal Body Passage every day. Then, the teaching effect would come out.

In addition, he could ask the big bosses about the cultivation techniques, medicinal herbs, treasures, heavenly flames, and other things needed to refine the immortal body. If it really didn’t work, he could contact the Almighty Merchant and borrow money from Senior White to buy it.

He would strive to let his disciples cultivate immortal bodies.

“Senior Yellow Mountain, do you want to walk through this passage?” Song Shuhang said.

Venerable Yellow Mountain shook his head. “Today’s target is mainly the treasures in the ruins. Let’s do it next time.’

“Alright, then I’ll take the seniors with me. The next time Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor want to use this immortal body passageway, contact me.” Song Shuhang said.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless.

He had a feeling that Shuhang was going to cause trouble.

“Let’s go, Senior.” Song Shuhang laughed, and stretched out his hand to carry Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor.

Then, he turned around and ran wildly in the Immortal Body Passage.

Mother Yellow Mountain, who was being carried on his back, was left with no dignity at all.

The total length of the immortal body passageway was only about two kilometers.

With Song Shuhangs speed, he would arrive in a blink of an eye.

After easily running out of the immortal body’s passageway, Song Shuhang flicked his finger and left the wooden saber in the passageway.

After he finished exploring the ruins, he would use the World Refining Holy Ape to dig out this precious passage. If possible, he could even consider moving the entire ruins to his Inner World.

In any case, his Inner World was constantly expanding, and there was a lot of empty space. He could move some ruins in and let his disciples and daughters play adventure games in the future.

Also, the members of the Nine Provinces Number One Group, such as Senior White and the playful Soft Feather, would definitely enjoy exploring these ruins.

“Alright, the passageway is out, Shuhang. Put us down.” Yellow Mountain said.

He was Venerable Yellow Mountain, but being carried on his shoulder while running was really damaging his image as a dignified senior.

On the other shoulder, Great Eastern Emperor’s eyes lit up.” This tunnel is indeed a shortcut. We passed five levels in one go and reached the sixth level! It saved us a lot of time!”

“Senior Yellow Mountain, there’s no hurry... Actually, I’m in a hurry this time. I’m still in a hurry to dig out the mysterious substance in the ruins that can upgrade treasures and upgrade my life-bound magical treasure. Next door, the Great Eastern Emperor of the ancient Heavenly City is still waiting to upgrade my magic weapon.” Song Shuhang said with a smile.

Yellow Mountain was confused.

Therefore, Senior Yellow Mountain, I’ll be the first to be rude this time!” Song Shuhang said.

After saying this much, he continued to carry Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor as he flew deeper into the ruins.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, be careful. The sixth layer is in front of you, and it has an incomparably terrifying sword qi array... This is also why I wanted to find a fellow daoist with a strong defense to resist.” Great Eastern Emperor shouted.

As he spoke, he felt a layer of armor intent defense on his body.

At the same time, Senior Tyrannical Songs body underwent many changes.

Two hundred holy apes appeared above Senior Tyrannical Songs head, singing hymns that he couldn’t understand. Senior Tyrannical Songs body was dyed black as if it was made of steel.

Then, Senior Tyrannical Song carried him and Yellow Mountain and entered the sixth level of the ruins.

The sword energy formation was triggered.

Countless terrifying sword qi burst forth and slashed towards them.

However, before the sword qi could reach them, it was all blocked by Senior Tyrannical Songs light of virtue.

Occasionally, one or two sword qi would break through the defense of the light of virtue, but Senior Tyrannical Song didn’t even look at them and directly collided with them.

The sword qi that troubled Great Eastern Emperor didn’t even leave a mark on Senior Tyrannical Songs pitch-black, metallic face. It couldn’t break through his defense at all.

The Sword Qi Formation and the exquisite attacks were not worth mentioning in the face of absolute strength.

In the blink of an eye, Song Shuhang broke through while carrying Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor.

The sixth level’s Sword Qi Array, the seventh level’s Five Elements Array, the eighth level’s Truth Attack, and the ninth level’s strange attack against the Essence Soul...

Tyrannical Song rammed through without using any extra spells.

In any case, on the way, every time they reached a stage, Great Eastern Emperor would shout, “Senior Tyrannical Song, be careful! There’s an XXXX attack ahead! ”

As soon as he finished speaking, he blinked his eyes and Tyrannical Song carried them to the next level.

This was a true boss!

When he reached the tenth level, which was the level of the ruins where the mysterious substance that enhanced the spiritual sense of the magic tool was located, Great Eastern Emperor was so emotional that he couldn’t speak.

To be honest, it was really too easy to explore the secret realm with Senior Tyrannical Song.

Previously, he had spent a few years to break through bit by bit before he reached the tenth level. Senior Tyrannical Song carried him and Yellow Mountain and arrived in a blink of an eye.

“This is the floor, Senior Tyrannical Song. The mysterious substance was hidden here. Senior, you can let us go now,” Great Eastern Emperor said.

“Haha.” Song Shuhang stretched out his hand and put Senior Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor down.

After Venerable Yellow Mountain was put down, he silently took out a bottle of pills and swallowed two of them.

His heart was still gratified, but he could not say anything.

In his memory, Song Shuhang had just joined the Nine Provinces Number One Group, and it was the first time he spoke in the group. The newbie’s appearance clearly felt like it was just yesterday, but it also felt like many years had passed...

Why did it seem like so many years had passed when it was only eight months

Chapter 2754: It’s Time to Unseal the Hidden Power in My Left Hand

Translator: EndlessFantasy Translation Editor: EndlessFantasy Translation

“Is this how it feels to be led by a big shot to clear the relic mystic realm?” Great Eastern Monarch sighed.

He had been lying down the entire way here.

No matter what kind of attack or trap they encountered in the secret realm, they were all insignificant in front of Tyrannical Song. Even if he accidentally fell into a trap, Big Boss Tyrannical Song only needed to speed up and run over it. Getting injured seemed so distant.

Along the way, Great Eastern Monarch also noticed that when some sword qi struck Big Boss Tyrannical Song’s body, it was all bounced back. Big Boss Tyrannical Song had his own passive defense and counterattack armor.

He and Yellow Mountain were carried on his shoulders from start to finish, arriving at their destination in the blink of an eye. The feeling of being led by a major big shot to clear the ruins was so exhilarating that he couldn’t speak.

Song Shuhang had finally become a true big shot, possessing the strength to instantly clear high-level instance dungeons with others. Although the number of instance dungeons he had cleared in his life was less than a fraction of those cleared by Yellow Mountain and Great Eastern Emperor, he didn’t have much experience. However, at this moment, experience was secondary. He just had to rush over.

“Monarch, where is the substance that can elevate the spirituality of a lifeblood magic treasure?” Song Shuhang’s enormous divine sense covered the entire tenth level of the Spirit Transformation Ruins.

However, he didn’t find the mysterious substance Great Eastern Monarch mentioned.

Moreover, the entire tenth level of the Spirit Transformation Ruins was empty. There were no hidden sword formations, no spell formation patterns, and no hidden secret chambers.

There was nothing but empty space.

“Senior Tyrannical Song, don’t be anxious. When I came back last time and finally managed to break into the tenth floor, I was also in despair when I saw the empty tenth floor. I spent several days carefully searching the first corner of the tenth floor. I didn’t even let go of a single brick, but I found nothing. At that time, my mentality collapsed,” Great Eastern Monarch laughed.

He had spent several years exploring this ruin, and in the end, he had finally made it to the tenth level, but there was not even a hair on his head. At that time, the despair in his heart was at least as big as three rooms, two halls, and two bathrooms.

“At that time, I didn’t get anything. It wasn’t easy for me to adjust my mentality and prepare to leave this Spirit Transformation Relic. Just as I was about to leave, a passage to the eleventh floor suddenly appeared in the empty tenth floor. At the same time, the substances that can increase the spirituality of the lifebound magic tool seeped out from the entrance of the eleventh floor,” Great Eastern Monarch explained.

Although it was common for cultivators to collapse after exploring ruins and finding nothing in the end, out of ten ruins, there would always be two or three of this type.

“Then where is the entrance to the eleventh floor?” Venerable Yellow Mountain asked.

“I don’t know.” Great Eastern Monarch suddenly shook his head.

Venerable Yellow Mountain was speechless.

“Last time, when the entrance to the eleventh floor suddenly opened, I couldn’t wait to barge in,” Dao Lord Li said, embarrassed. “In the end, when I entered the eleventh level, I didn’t even see what was on the eleventh level clearly... I suffered a heavy blow. It was as if a huge meteorite had smashed into my head, directly knocking me unconscious and sending me back to the tenth level. I

was in the tenth floor tor over ten months.”

If it wasn’t for the fact that his cultivation was strong enough, he would have died long ago after being unconscious for ten months.

“The only thing I can confirm is that the attack method of the eleventh floor is a very evil type of attack, combined with physical attacks. After I woke up, the reward I received was a portion of the ‘mysterious substance’ that seeped out from the eleventh floor when it opened. That’s why I want to go deeper into the Spirit Transformation Vestige. I want to find fellow daoists with strong defenses and eminent monks with great merit to help me break through to the eleventh level,” Great Eastern Monarch said.

The enormous power of virtue dispelled the evil energy, and the fellow daoists with strong defensive abilities withstood the physical attack.

“Then how do we get to the eleventh floor?” Song Shuhang asked.

“Wait!” Dao Lord Li said seriously. “There must be an opportunity for the eleventh floor to open. It will open at a certain time. At this time, we only need to wait patiently. Moreover, this opportunity will not be too long. At most, it will be activated once a month. When I woke up last time, I found traces of the mysterious substance leaking from ten locations.”

This also meant that the coordinates of the eleventh floor were not fixed, but randomly opened.

Song Shuhang raised his head and looked at the sky. “In other words, if we’re unlucky, we’ll have to wait here for a month?”

“It’s only a month. It’s just a little time for us to get a seat,” Great Eastern Monarch said.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

I can do a lot of things in a month. Perhaps he could even meet the big shot of the heavenly tribulation again.

Besides, I’m in a hurry.

The Great Eastern Emperor next door is still waiting to upgrade my equipment. How can I wait so long?

“Shuhang, are you in a hurry?” Venerable Yellow Mountain asked.

“Yes, so... I’ll have to ask Senior White to lend me a hand,” Song Shuhang said.

Chapter 2775: Should I Secretly Cheat Halfway Through?

It’s so cool to steal lines, just like the cool summer.

Should I secretly cheat halfway?

The tentacles on his face were filled with despair.

“No problem, Senior!” Song Shuhang said heroically.

At this moment, Fairy Feng Yi, who was sitting quietly on his shoulder, suddenly thought of something and asked, “By the way, will you be able to control the process of randomly drawing cards? After all, this black box is your magic tool, right?”

However, as soon as she finished speaking, her claws trembled in fear, and she thought to herself. “How dare I talk back to the ruler of the Netherworld! Am I being arrogant?”

Although this ruler of the Netherworld might be very approachable, it still depended on the person he was with. What if he was unhappy and secretly cursed her? The ruler of the Netherworld was best at scheming in the dark.

“You can rest assured about this... My bet ceremony is fair. In other words, I can achieve this basic level of fairness with a hundred percent certainty. Even if it’s my magic tool, it’s 100% random when it comes to drawing cards,” the three-eyed youth replied.

Fairness on the surface meant that the most basic choices had to be fair and flawless.

“Don’t worry, Fairy Feng Yi. Under Senior White’s hand... Even if I randomly draw it, it will definitely be a card of the highest level,” Song Shuhang said confidently.

Fairy Feng Yi was infected by the confidence of the masked fellow Daoist, Shuhang.

“He’s here! One round to decide the winner.” Song Shuhang’s aura was like a rainbow. He raised his white hand high and slapped it down!

Just as he was about to hit the black box, he retracted all the strength in his arm and pressed it gently on the black box.

Fairy Feng Yi was speechless.

She felt that it would be better if Shuhang didn’t have so much passion. He slapped it hard and landed lightly, giving people the feeling that he was a coward.

You still fell for it, little friend Tyrannical Song... The trap laid by “fair on the surface” was to “use the number of laws” to determine the winner!

The more nomological laws a card had, the more precious it might not be!

There were even many six-rule cards that needed more rules to make up for the lack of materials.

Breaking the law?

Iron Fist of Punishment?

Before the fist could move, the space around the fist had already cracked from the power of the fist. There were even some of the laws of destruction of the ruler of the Netherworld that began to condense.

“You just want to find an excuse to beat me up.” Song Shuhang said. The holy ape appeared behind him, and the four great body-tempering techniques circulated, directly raising his physique by a level.

Not only that, but Song Shuhang also mobilized the holy light in his body and used it on his body. At the very least, he wanted to disgust the three-eyed young senior.

Come on, hurt each other!

Under the premise that his physical fitness and realm were suppressed to the same level, fighting each other was advantageous to him. If he was injured by 800, the three-eyed youth would have to lose at least 1,000!

800 for 1000, he made a small profit.

Senior Three-Eyed’s ‘Ruler of the Netherworld’s Destruction Law’ could only strengthen his aura a little.

The ruler of the Netherworld!

As Immortals, even if some of them had never seen the ruler of the Netherworld with their own eyes, they would still know of its existence and its special nature.

This evil energy of the Netherworld, which far surpassed that of ordinary Immortals, was an existence that surpassed Immortals, and it was half of the Heavenly Dao.

Moreover... Didn’t the Heavenly Dao collapse?

Why did the ruler of the Netherworld still exist?

What was the secret behind this?

And why was Tyrannical Song with this ruler of the Netherworld?

Boom ~ The three-eyed ruler of the Netherworld seemed to be very angry. He waved his fist and smashed it toward Tyrannical Song.

When this punch was thrown, it was accompanied by the terrifying Laws of Destruction of the ruler of the Netherworld, the purest and most violent destruction.

Just this terrifying law of destruction was enough to move the Immortals.

No one was willing to take a punch from the ruler of the Netherworld that was filled with the laws of destruction!

Even for Immortals, when faced with such a punch, their best option would be to dodge.

However, how could it be so easy to dodge the fist of the ruler of the Netherworld?

The Immortals could sense that the Three-Eyed Hegemon’s fist contained the nomological law of ‘Karma Lockdown.’

When the fist was thrown, there was no way to dodge it-it was destined to land on Tyrannical Song!

Was Tyrannical Song a monster?

He retaliated!

Holy Light, Power of Virtue, Heavenly Lightning Proof, Holy Ape Enhancement, Scholarly Morality Enhancement...

I don’t believe that all B’s are wrong!

Just my ass!

Still talented?

Do you have some misunderstanding about the difficulty of cultivators’ advancement?

However, Song Shuhang’s intuition told him that the other party might have seen through his acting.

‘Did I give myself away somewhere?’ As Song Shuhang shouted, he awkwardly stopped. The other party had already seen through him, and if he continued to shout, he would feel like a fool.

‘Scream, continue screaming!’ A message was transmitted from the big-eyed planet.

Song Shuhang was speechless.

‘I almost let you fool me. I won’t give you the chance to act anymore. I want to give you the greatest pain.’ The big-eyed planet sent a message.

Its mental energy locked onto Song Shuhang, and a new eye technique condensed in its huge eyes—the Dissolving Demon Eye, also known as the Thousand Chopping Demon Eye.

Since Tyrannical Song liked to split up, it would satisfy him.

‘How did you find out that I was acting?’ Song Shuhang asked slowly. He was very good at acting, and his screams were very accurate. He even split his body open and suppressed his aura without any flaws.

The big-eyed planet’s pupils lit up. It didn’t want to answer Song Shuhang, nor did it want to talk nonsense. It just wanted to tear Tyrannical Song’s body into pieces.

In a situation where one party did not want to chat at all, they naturally could not continue chatting.

‘Madam Long Luo, are you still not done?’ Song Shuhang said anxiously.

The big-eyed planet was going to exert its strength. If he continued to be passively beaten, he would really have to taste the pain.

However, Madam Long Luo didn’t immediately reply to Song Shuhang.

‘Ms. Chubby Ball ~ I can’t hold on anymore.’ Song Shuhang quickly changed the way he addressed her.

‘Right now.’ Madam Long Luo replied, ‘Give me the golden core’s QR code!’

‘You can already add me as a friend?’ Song Shuhang asked. At the same time, he quickly took out the ‘Golden Core QR code’ and enlarged it, allowing it to shine in the eyes of the big-eyed planet boss.

The big-eyed planet’s boss’s gaze and mental energy were locked on Song Shuhang.

As soon as the golden core’s QR code was swiped, its mental power subconsciously swiped over it.

‘Ding  You have added Tyrannical Song as a friend and have been added to the ‘Blacklist 2,’ nickname: Big Eyeball. I wish you a happy life.’

The big-eyed planet was confused.

What the hell was this?

Before it could react, Tyrannical Song on the other side made a new move.

A divine eye opened on Tyrannical Song’s forehead.

This divine third eye had the aura of its master, which had a strong restraining effect on it.

‘Send the information of my newly weaved program to it!’ Madam Long Luo warned.

She had been modifying the ‘client program’ into a ‘virus-type’ program.

The big-eyed planet boss could indeed become the most perfect server carrier for the ‘cultivation’ function client. However, she and Song Shuhang didn’t need to subdue the big-eyed planet’s big shot and take him as a pet.

They only needed a portion of the big-eyed planet boss’s memory as the server for the client download.

Therefore, he only needed to launch the ‘client program’ into the big-eyed planet’s body and use the authority of the ‘divine third eye’ to solidify the program.

Next, he could send the big-eyed planet away...

‘Ms. Chubby Ball, you are awesome ~’ Song Shuhang tried his best to flatter her. At the same time, his divine third eye flashed, and a ray of light shot into the big-eyed planet’s big shot’s pupil.

As for Madam Long Luo, she cooperated with Song Shuhang and used the ‘friend private chat’ function to send the other part of the ‘cultivation chat program fixed patch package’ directly to the big-eyed planet.
